## הֲ (id: 001736000000000)

הֲ
==

הֲ

inter

Affirmers

?, whether marker denoting that the truth value of the following statement is under investigation

## הָבְנִים (id: 001744000000000)

הָבְנִים
========

הָבְנִים (H1894) — הֹובְנִים

noun m

Trees

ebony \= a spiny tree up to 6–7 m. high; its leaves are compound, with the leaflets nearly opposite one another on the spine; it grows white flowers that hang in loose clusters, that give way to flat, papery seedpods about 6 cm long and 1 cm wide; found in Africa and locally known as zebrawood; ◄ Dalbergia melanoxylon; alternatively: \= a tree which grows to 10 m. tall, with evergreen leaves; the inner part of its trunk is black; it is found in India and Sri Lanka: ◄ Diospyros ebenum; ► used by carvers, who inlay the wood with ivory

[EZK 27:15](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:15)1

1 EZK 27:15 MT\-K והובנִים \| MT\-Q וְהָבְנִים

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Ezekiel 27:15

1 ISA 16:7 NIV "the men" follows LXX (τοις κατοικουσιν) and makes the text cohere with JER 48:31, which has אַנְשֵׁי ("men") instead of the אַשִׁישֵׁי ("raisin cakes")

Move

to lead, to take, to bring \= causative action or process by which humans or deities cause (other) humans or objects to move forward, usually towards a specific destination

Act

to make go, to lead \= causative process by which humans cause other humans to follow a certain pattern of behavior, ◄ which is described as their journey through life

[PRO 16:29](https://ref.ly/Prov16:29)

Afraid

**Collocation:** בִּרְכַּיִם הלך מַיִם

to lose courage literally: (one's) knees turn to water; hence: \= to lose (one's) courage

[EZK 7:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek7:17) · [EZK 21:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:12)

Alive

to go \> to live literally: to go; hence: \= process by which living creatures live their life until the moment of death

Dead

to pass away \= process by which someone is going to die, described as a movement in one way only

Non\-Exist

to vanish \= process by which an object vanishes from existence

Happen

to happen \= process by which events take place, ◄ as if they move like objects

End

to leave, to be over literally: to go away; hence: \= process by which an event stops happening

[JOB 16:6](https://ref.ly/Job16:6) · [SNG 2:11](https://ref.ly/Song2:11)

End

**Collocation:** הלך חֶרְפָּה

to bring (one's) shame \> to hide (one's) disgrace literally: to bring (one's) shame; \= causative process by which humans deal with their shame

[2SA 13:13](https://ref.ly/2Sam13:13)

Flee

**Collocation:** הלך אֶל־נֶפֶשׁ

to run for (one's) life literally: to go to (one's) life; hence: \= action by which humans move away from a certain place in order to save their life from danger

[1KI 19:3](https://ref.ly/1Kgs19:3)

Endure

to go on \= process by which events continue over a prolonged period of time, ◄ described as movement along time

People

Serve

Sex

**Collocation:** הלך אֶל

to go to \> have sex with \= action by which humans approach (other) humans for having sexual relations

Space

to extend to \= state in which something exists in space, of which the existence is described as a movement from one place to another

## הֲלָךְ (id: 001825000000000)

הֲלָךְ
======

הֲלָךְ (A1983)

noun m

Objects

tax exact meaning unsure; probably: \= an amount of money that is to be paid to a ruler in return for certain rights or privileges

[EZR 4:13](https://ref.ly/Ezra4:13) · [EZR 4:20](https://ref.ly/Ezra4:20) · [EZR 7:24](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:24)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Ezra 4:13; Ezra 4:20; Ezra 7:24


## הֵלֶךְ (id: 001826000000000)

הֵלֶךְ
======

הֵלֶךְ (H1982)

noun m · הלך

Flow

flow \= process by which a liquid flows from a certain place

[1SA 14:26](https://ref.ly/1Sam14:26)

People

traveler \= person who is on a journey from one place to another

[2SA 12:4](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:4)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** 1 Samuel 14:26; 2 Samuel 12:4

הלל
===

הלל (H1984)

verb · אהל · הֵילֵל

Shine

to shine, to flash forth, to emit (light) \= process by which an object emits or reflects light; ≈ regarded as awesome

[JOB 29:3](https://ref.ly/Job29:3) · [JOB 31:26](https://ref.ly/Job31:26) · [JOB 41:10](https://ref.ly/Job41:10) · [ISA 13:10](https://ref.ly/Isa13:10)

verb · הִלּוּלִים · מַהֲלָל · תְּהִלָּה · הִלֵּל · מַהֲלַלְאֵל

Praise

to praise, to give praise \= action by which humans or divine beings express their appreciation, admiration, respect, and/or gratitude to (other) humans or deities about who they are and what they do

Great

to boast, to brag \= action by which humans express their pride and satisfaction about themselves, their actions, certain circumstances they find themselves in, or a deity that they consider responsible for those circumstances

Rejoice

to exult \= state in which humans experience great joy and act accordingly

Foolish

folly \= state in which an action is regarded as abnormal and associated with people who are insane

[ECC 2:2](https://ref.ly/Eccl2:2)

Foolish

to behave madly, to go mad \= action by which humans act in a way that is regarded as abnormal and associated with people who are insane

[1SA 21:14](https://ref.ly/1Sam21:14) · [JER 25:16](https://ref.ly/Jer25:16) · [JER 50:38](https://ref.ly/Jer50:38) · [JER 51:7](https://ref.ly/Jer51:7)

Foolish

to make a fool of \= causative action by which deities or humans cause (other) humans to either become fools or look like fools

[JOB 12:17](https://ref.ly/Job12:17) · [PSA 102:9](https://ref.ly/Ps102:9) · [ECC 7:7](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:7) · [ISA 44:25](https://ref.ly/Isa44:25)

Urge

to rage, to charge madly, to dash wildly \= action by which vehicles move at a larger speed than is considered responsible, ≈ which is associated with insane behavior

[JER 46:9](https://ref.ly/Jer46:9) · [NAM 2:5](https://ref.ly/Nah2:5)

## הִלֵּל (id: 001828000000000)

הִלֵּל
======

הִלֵּל (H1985)

name · הלל

Names of People

Hillel \= man; ► father of Abdon, judge

[JDG 12:13](https://ref.ly/Judg12:13) · [JDG 12:15](https://ref.ly/Judg12:15)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Judges 12:13; Judges 12:15


## הלם (id: 001829000000000)

הלם
===

הלם (H1986)

verb · הַלְמוּת · מַהֲלֻמֹות

Impact

to strike, to smash \= action by which humans or animals deliver a blow to an object with their hands, whether or not with the help of an instrument such as a hammer, or with their feet

[JDG 5:22](https://ref.ly/Judg5:22) · [JDG 5:26](https://ref.ly/Judg5:26) · [PSA 74:6](https://ref.ly/Ps74:6) · [PSA 141:5](https://ref.ly/Ps141:5) · [PRO 23:35](https://ref.ly/Prov23:35) · [ISA 41:7](https://ref.ly/Isa41:7)

Weak

to beat, to make numb, to overcome \= causative action by which alcoholic drinks have a numbing effect on humans, comparable to being beaten by a hammer

[ISA 16:8](https://ref.ly/Isa16:8)1 · [ISA 28:1](https://ref.ly/Isa28:1)

1 ISA 16:8 NJB "overcome" NRSV GNT "made drunk" REB "overpower" \| RSV ESV "struck down" NIV "trample" \| NJPS "spread"

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Judges 5:22; Judges 5:26; Psalms 74:6; Psalms 141:5; Proverbs 23:35; Isaiah 41:7; Isaiah 16:8; Isaiah 28:1


## הֲלֹם (id: 001830000000000)

הֲלֹם
=====

הֲלֹם (H1988)

adv

Spatial Referents

here \= a reference to the location of the speaker

[GEN 16:13](https://ref.ly/Gen16:13) · [EXO 3:5](https://ref.ly/Exod3:5) · [JDG 18:3](https://ref.ly/Judg18:3) · [JDG 20:7](https://ref.ly/Judg20:7) · [RUT 2:14](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:14) · [1SA 10:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:22) · [1SA 14:36](https://ref.ly/1Sam14:36) · [1SA 14:38](https://ref.ly/1Sam14:38) · [PSA 73:10](https://ref.ly/Ps73:10)

Spatial Referents

in all directions, hither and tither \= a reference to an imprecise location away from the speaker

[1SA 14:16](https://ref.ly/1Sam14:16)

Temporal Referents

**Collocation:** עַד־הַלֹם

thus far \= a reference to the present as the temporary endpoint of an event begun in the past

[2SA 7:18](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:18) · [1CH 17:16](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:16)

1 For a discussion of problems, see Hossfeld/Senger

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 16:13; Exodus 3:5; Judges 18:3; Judges 20:7; Ruth 2:14; 1 Samuel 10:22; 1 Samuel 14:36; 1 Samuel 14:38; Psalms 73:10; 1 Samuel 14:16; 2 Samuel 7:18; 1 Chronicles 17:16

## הַלְמוּת (id: 001832000000000)

הַלְמוּת
========

הַלְמוּת (H1989)

noun f · הלם

Tools

**Collocation:** הַלְמוּת עַמֵלִים

hammer \= instrument of about 30 centimeters long, consisting of a handle, usually made of wood, to which was attached a stone, wooden, or (less frequently) metal head; ► used for many purposes, including the breaking or dressing of building stones, pounding nails or pegs into wood, or pounding pegs into the ground; also used by blacksmiths to shape hot metal

[JDG 5:26](https://ref.ly/Judg5:26)

Reinier de Blois; Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Judges 5:26

## המה (id: 001836000000000)

המה
===

המה (H1993)

verb · הֵמֶה · הָמֹון · הֶמְיָה · הָם

Sounds

to moan, to groan, to roar, to growl \= action by which humans, animals, or objects produce a variety of sounds, often associated with animals, but also with natural phenomena like the waves of a stormy sea

[PSA 42:6](https://ref.ly/Ps42:6) · [PSA 42:12](https://ref.ly/Ps42:12) · [PSA 43:5](https://ref.ly/Ps43:5) · [PSA 46:4](https://ref.ly/Ps46:4) · [PSA 46:7](https://ref.ly/Ps46:7) · [PSA 55:18](https://ref.ly/Ps55:18) · [PSA 59:7](https://ref.ly/Ps59:7) · [PSA 59:15](https://ref.ly/Ps59:15) · [PSA 77:4](https://ref.ly/Ps77:4) · [PSA 83:3](https://ref.ly/Ps83:3) · [SNG 5:4](https://ref.ly/Song5:4) · [ISA 16:11](https://ref.ly/Isa16:11) · [ISA 17:12](https://ref.ly/Isa17:12) · [ISA 17:12](https://ref.ly/Isa17:12) · [ISA 51:15](https://ref.ly/Isa51:15) · [ISA 59:11](https://ref.ly/Isa59:11) · [JER 4:19](https://ref.ly/Jer4:19) · [JER 5:22](https://ref.ly/Jer5:22) · [JER 6:23](https://ref.ly/Jer6:23) · [JER 31:20](https://ref.ly/Jer31:20) · [JER 31:35](https://ref.ly/Jer31:35) · [JER 48:36](https://ref.ly/Jer48:36) · [JER 48:36](https://ref.ly/Jer48:36) · [JER 50:42](https://ref.ly/Jer50:42) · [JER 51:55](https://ref.ly/Jer51:55) · [EZK 7:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek7:16)

Speak

to be in tumult, to be in uproar, to be loud \= action by which humans speak loudly, ≈ often associated with a lack of wisdom

[1KI 1:41](https://ref.ly/1Kgs1:41) · [PSA 39:7](https://ref.ly/Ps39:7) · [PRO 7:11](https://ref.ly/Prov7:11) · [PRO 9:13](https://ref.ly/Prov9:13) · [PRO 20:1](https://ref.ly/Prov20:1) · [ISA 22:2](https://ref.ly/Isa22:2) · [ZEC 9:15](https://ref.ly/Zech9:15)

Towns

noisy (streets) \= state in which the traffic in streets makes much noise

[PRO 1:21](https://ref.ly/Prov1:21)

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 42:6; Psalms 42:12; Psalms 43:5; Psalms 46:4; Psalms 46:7; Psalms 55:18; Psalms 59:7; Psalms 59:15; Psalms 77:4; Psalms 83:3; Song of Songs 5:4; Isaiah 16:11; Isaiah 17:12; Isaiah 51:15; Isaiah 59:11; Jeremiah 4:19; Jeremiah 5:22; Jeremiah 6:23; Jeremiah 31:20; Jeremiah 31:35; Jeremiah 48:36; Jeremiah 50:42; Jeremiah 51:55; Ezekiel 7:16; 1 Kings 1:41; Psalms 39:7; Proverbs 7:11; Proverbs 9:13; Proverbs 20:1; Isaiah 22:2; Zechariah 9:15; Proverbs 1:21


## הֵמֶה (id: 001837000000000)

הֵמֶה
=====

הֵמֶה (H1991)

noun m · המה

Quantity

wealth \= state in which humans possess a large quantity of goods

[EZK 7:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek7:11)1

1 EZK 7:11 The interpretation of this verse is difficult; perhaps REB is on the right track by understanding the second part as a series of questions. This way הֵמֶה could be explained as from המה with the meaning "tumult".

Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Ezekiel 7:11

## הפך (id: 001859000000000)

הפך
===

הפך (H2015)

verb · הֵפֶךְ · הֲפֵכָה · הֲפַכְפַּךְ · מַהְפֵּכָה · מַהְפֶּכֶת · תַּהְפֻּכֹות

Turn

to turn, to turn around, to turn back \= action by which humans turn their body around in order to face a different direction than before

[JOS 8:20](https://ref.ly/Josh8:20) · [JDG 20:39](https://ref.ly/Judg20:39) · [JDG 20:41](https://ref.ly/Judg20:41) · [1SA 25:12](https://ref.ly/1Sam25:12) · [2KI 5:26](https://ref.ly/2Kgs5:26) · [2CH 9:12](https://ref.ly/2Chr9:12) · [PSA 78:9](https://ref.ly/Ps78:9) · [EZK 4:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek4:8)

Turn

**Collocation:** הפך עֹרֶף

to turn (one's) back (to flee) literally: to turn one's neck; hence: \= action by which humans turn around in order to flee

[JOS 7:8](https://ref.ly/Josh7:8)

Turn

to overturn \= causative action by which humans or deities turn an object upside down

[2KI 21:13](https://ref.ly/2Kgs21:13) · [HOS 7:8](https://ref.ly/Hos7:8)

Turn · Impact

to overturn \= causative action by which forces or deities forcefully remove an object from its place and turn it upside down, which implies destruction

[JDG 7:13](https://ref.ly/Judg7:13) · [JOB 9:5](https://ref.ly/Job9:5) · [JOB 28:9](https://ref.ly/Job28:9)

Turn

**Collocation:** הפך יָד

to turn (a chariot) literally: to turn (one's) hand(s); hence: \= causative action by which a charioteer causes his vehicle to turn around giving a firm pull on the reins of the horse

[1KI 22:34](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:34) · [2KI 9:23](https://ref.ly/2Kgs9:23) · [2CH 18:33](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:33)

Turn · Move

to turn, to whirl, to swirl around \= process by which objects move into a certain direction while turning around their axis

[GEN 3:24](https://ref.ly/Gen3:24) · [JDG 7:13](https://ref.ly/Judg7:13) · [JOB 37:12](https://ref.ly/Job37:12)

Change

to change \= process by which events take on a different nature

[EXO 14:5](https://ref.ly/Exod14:5) · [EST 9:1](https://ref.ly/Esth9:1) · [EST 9:22](https://ref.ly/Esth9:22) · [PSA 32:4](https://ref.ly/Ps32:4) · [LAM 1:20](https://ref.ly/Lam1:20) · [LAM 5:15](https://ref.ly/Lam5:15) · [DAN 10:8](https://ref.ly/Dan10:8) · [HOS 11:8](https://ref.ly/Hos11:8)

Change

to change \= causative process by which humans or deities give events a different nature

[DEU 23:6](https://ref.ly/Deut23:6) · [NEH 13:2](https://ref.ly/Neh13:2) · [JOB 34:25](https://ref.ly/Job34:25)1 · [PSA 30:12](https://ref.ly/Ps30:12) · [PSA 41:4](https://ref.ly/Ps41:4) · [PSA 105:25](https://ref.ly/Ps105:25) · [JER 23:36](https://ref.ly/Jer23:36) · [JER 31:13](https://ref.ly/Jer31:13) · [AMO 5:7](https://ref.ly/Amos5:7) · [AMO 5:8](https://ref.ly/Amos5:8) · [AMO 6:12](https://ref.ly/Amos6:12) · [AMO 8:10](https://ref.ly/Amos8:10) · [ZEP 3:9](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:9)

Chastise

**Collocation:** הפך יָד

to punish literally: to turn (one's) hand (to); hence: \= action by which deities punish humans

[LAM 3:3](https://ref.ly/Lam3:3)

Different

to change, to turn into, to become \= process by which humans, deities, or objects take on a different nature, character, or form

[EXO 7:15](https://ref.ly/Exod7:15) · [EXO 7:17](https://ref.ly/Exod7:17) · [EXO 7:20](https://ref.ly/Exod7:20) · [LEV 13:3](https://ref.ly/Lev13:3) · [LEV 13:4](https://ref.ly/Lev13:4) · [LEV 13:13](https://ref.ly/Lev13:13) · [LEV 13:16](https://ref.ly/Lev13:16) · [LEV 13:17](https://ref.ly/Lev13:17) · [LEV 13:20](https://ref.ly/Lev13:20) · [LEV 13:25](https://ref.ly/Lev13:25) · [1SA 10:6](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:6) · [JOB 19:19](https://ref.ly/Job19:19) · [JOB 20:14](https://ref.ly/Job20:14) · [JOB 28:5](https://ref.ly/Job28:5) · [JOB 30:21](https://ref.ly/Job30:21) · [JOB 38:14](https://ref.ly/Job38:14) · [JOB 41:20](https://ref.ly/Job41:20) · [PSA 78:57](https://ref.ly/Ps78:57) · [PRO 17:20](https://ref.ly/Prov17:20) · [ISA 34:9](https://ref.ly/Isa34:9) · [ISA 63:10](https://ref.ly/Isa63:10) · [JER 2:21](https://ref.ly/Jer2:21) · [JER 30:6](https://ref.ly/Jer30:6) · [JOL 3:4](https://ref.ly/Joel3:4)

Different

to change, to turn into \= causative process by which humans, deities, or forces give (other) humans or objects a different nature, character, or form

[EXO 10:19](https://ref.ly/Exod10:19) · [LEV 13:10](https://ref.ly/Lev13:10) · [1SA 10:9](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:9) · [PSA 66:6](https://ref.ly/Ps66:6) · [PSA 78:44](https://ref.ly/Ps78:44) · [PSA 105:29](https://ref.ly/Ps105:29) · [PSA 114:8](https://ref.ly/Ps114:8) · [JER 13:23](https://ref.ly/Jer13:23)

Different

**Collocation:** הפך עַיִן

to change (its) appearance literally: to change (its) appearance; hence: \= process by which an object starts to look differently

[LEV 13:55](https://ref.ly/Lev13:55)

Impact

to overthrow, to destroy \= causative action by which humans or deities destroy an object completely ◄ as if by turning it completely upside down

Happen

הֶרֶס

1 ISA 19:18 This expression probably is a pun on the name of the Egyptian town of Heliopolis, which, translated into Hebrew, would be עִיר הַחֶרֶס \| MT NIV "City of Destruction" \| LXX Πόλισ\-ασεδεκ \| NJPS "Town of Heres" \| 1QIsa Vul σ´ HOTTP\-B RSV NJB NRSV REB GNT CEV "City of the Sun"
